869<h1 class="m-detail-header--title">

870Cannabidiol Industry Gets High, Expected to Hit $2 Billion by 2022</h1>

871<div class="m-detail-header--dek">

872The cannabidiol (CBD) industry is growing fast, according to new data, with sales of hemp-derived CBD now surpassing that for marijuana-derived CBD.</div>

873<div class="m-detail-header--meta">

874<div class="m-description--list">

875<div class="m-description--term">

876Author:</div>

877<div class="m-description--details m-detail-header--meta-item">

878<a class="m-detail-header--meta-author" href="/author/katherine-ross" onclick="return phoenixTrackClickEvent(this, event);" phx-track-id="Author Name" rel="author">

879Katherine Ross</a>

880</div>

881</div>

882</div>

939<p>

940Lift off.</p>

941<p>

942The cannabidiol (CBD) industry is expected to be worth $2 billion by 2022 according to new data from New Frontier Data.&#xA0;</p>

943<p>

944In 2017, the CBD industry grew by 40% and hit $367 million in sales. Don&apos;t get CBD confused with <a href="https://www.thestreet.com/lifestyle/what-is-thc-14655181">

945THC</a>

946, however, the <a href="https://www.thestreet.com/lifestyle/difference-between-cbd-vs-thc-14627877">

947two are different</a>

948. CBD without THC <a href="https://www.thestreet.com/lifestyle/health/what-is-cbd-14578964">

949won&apos;t get you high</a>

950.&#xA0;</p>

951<ul>

952<li>

953Why Canopy Growth Is the &apos;Blue Chip of Pot Stocks&apos;</li>

954</ul>

955<p>

956For the first time, CBD derived from hemp surged ahead of marijuana-derived CBD in 2017. New Frontier expects &quot;to see continued changes as the pharmaceutical sector officially opens in 2018.&quot;</p>

1086<p>

1087By 2022, the hemp-derived CBD market is expected to be worth $646 million, while the marijuana-derived market will grow to $647 million.</p>

1088<ul>

1089<li>

1090<a href="https://www.thestreet.com/video/california-exploding-cannabis-industry-has-a-surprising-problem-with-cash-14673052">

1091California&apos;s Exploding Cannabis Industry Has a Surprising Problem With Cash</a>

1092</li>

1093</ul>

1094<p>

1095This year, CBD products reached $367 million in sales and New Frontier expects the market to be worth $1.2 billion by 2020.&#xA0;</p>

1096<p>

1097According to the data, over 25,500 acres of land were devoted to growing hemp in 2017. The hemp was grown in 19 states and the majority, 70%, was devoted to CBD.&#xA0;</p>

1115&quot;The U.S. CBD market is primed for expansive growth across its three primary sectors, hemp-derived CBD, marijuana-derived CBD and pharmaceutical CBD...We project that by 2022, each of these three sectors will account for approximately one-third of the $1.9 billion total market,&quot; said Giadha Aguirre de Carcer, CEO of New Frontier Data.</p>
